Here is the comprehensive architecture:\\n\\n## Role Definition Hierarchy\\nThe base role definitions are in `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go` which defines the `RoleType` enum with four values: RoleNone, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, and RoleAdmin. These are re-exported in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for organizational context.\\n\\n## Permission Types\\n`pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go` defines three permission levels as bit flags:\\n- PERMISSION_VIEW (1 << 0) - Read-only access\\n- PERMISSION_EDIT (1 << 1) - Write/modify access\\n- PERMISSION_ADMIN (1 << 2) - Admin access including permission management\\n\\n## ACL Models\\n`pkg/services/dashboards/models.go` contains the `DashboardACL` struct which maps these permission types to users, teams, and roles. Permission data flows through `pkg/api/dtos/acl.go` which defines `UpdateDashboardACLCommand` and related DTOs.\\n\\n## Action-to-Permission Mapping\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go` defines action constants (ActionFoldersRead, ActionFoldersWrite, ActionDashboardsRead, ActionDashboardsWrite, etc.) that represent granular permission operations.\\n\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go` maps the three role tiers to sets of actions:\\n- DashboardViewActions: includes ActionDashboardsRead\\n- DashboardEditActions: extends ViewActions with ActionDashboardsWrite, ActionDashboardsDelete\\n- DashboardAdminActions: extends EditActions with ActionDashboardsPermissionsRead, ActionDashboardsPermissionsWrite\\n\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go` follows the same pattern for folder permissions:\\n- FolderViewActions: ActionFoldersRead\\n- FolderEditActions: extends ViewActions with ActionFoldersWrite, ActionFoldersDelete\\n- FolderAdminActions: extends EditActions with ActionFoldersPermissionsRead, ActionFoldersPermissionsWrite\\n\\n## Role Registration and Built-in Roles\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` contains `GetBuiltinRoles()` which registers fixed roles for Admin, Editor, and Viewer with their associated permission sets. These are referenced throughout the codebase.\\n\\n## Permission Enforcement Middleware\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go` provides the `Middleware()` function that acts as a permission guard for HTTP endpoints. It evaluates whether a user has required permissions before allowing access.\\n\\n`pkg/middleware/auth.go` provides additional auth middleware functions like `SnapshotPublicModeOrCreate` and `SnapshotPublicModeOrDelete` that enforce specific permission checks.\\n\\n## Permissions Service Interface\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go` defines the `PermissionsService`, `FolderPermissionsService`, and `DashboardPermissionsService` interfaces. These services are implemented in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go` with methods:\\n- SetUserPermission: assigns a permission to a specific user\\n- SetTeamPermission: assigns a permission to a team\\n- SetBuiltInRolePermission: assigns a permission to a built-in role (Viewer/Editor/Admin)\\n\\nThe API layer in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/api.go` exposes HTTP endpoints for managing these permissions.\\n\\n## Folder and Dashboard Permissions APIs\\n`pkg/api/dashboard_permission.go` and `pkg/api/folder_permission.go` provide HTTP endpoints to:\\n- Get permissions (using folder/dashboard-specific permission service)\\n- Update permissions with validation\\n- Convert permission objects for API responses\\n\\n## Permission Inheritance\\n`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go` contains the critical `GetInheritedScopes()` function which implements permission inheritance from parent folders to child dashboards and subfolders. This function queries the folder service to get ancestors and builds a chain of inherited permission scopes.\\n\\n`pkg/services/searchV2/auth.go` uses inherited scopes for search result filtering, checking permissions across the folder hierarchy.\\n\\n`pkg/api/annotations.go` applies inherited scopes when resolving permissions for annotations linked to dashboards.\\n\\n## Folder Hierarchy Support\\n`pkg/services/folder/service.go` and `pkg/services/folder/model.go` provide folder hierarchy operations. The folder service's `GetParents()` method is used by `GetInheritedScopes()` to walk up the folder tree and collect inherited permission scopes.\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to:\\n1. Define granular permission actions mapped to three role tiers\\n2. Enforce permissions via middleware on all endpoints\\n3. Allow per-resource permission overrides for users, teams, and basic roles\\n4. Inherit permissions from parent folders to contained resources\\n5. Validate and update permissions through a centralized permissions service\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":350,"cache_read_input_tokens":106175,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":350},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e2fb3a36-5ad3-42da-b37a-727bcc1ecf8b","uuid":"25536d56-d627-4715-85e6-437a36f7c3f7"}

These are referenced throughout the codebase.\\n\\n## Permission Enforcement Middleware\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go` provides the `Middleware()` function that acts as a permission guard for HTTP endpoints. It evaluates whether a user has required permissions before allowing access.\\n\\n`pkg/middleware/auth.go` provides additional auth middleware functions like `SnapshotPublicModeOrCreate` and `SnapshotPublicModeOrDelete` that enforce specific permission checks.\\n\\n## Permissions Service Interface\\n`pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go` defines the `PermissionsService`, `FolderPermissionsService`, and `DashboardPermissionsService` interfaces. These services are implemented in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go` with methods:\\n- SetUserPermission: assigns a permission to a specific user\\n- SetTeamPermission: assigns a permission to a team\\n- SetBuiltInRolePermission: assigns a permission to a built-in role (Viewer/Editor/Admin)\\n\\nThe API layer in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/api.go` exposes HTTP endpoints for managing these permissions.\\n\\n## Folder and Dashboard Permissions APIs\\n`pkg/api/dashboard_permission.go` and `pkg/api/folder_permission.go` provide HTTP endpoints to:\\n- Get permissions (using folder/dashboard-specific permission service)\\n- Update permissions with validation\\n- Convert permission objects for API responses\\n\\n## Permission Inheritance\\n`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go` contains the critical `GetInheritedScopes()` function which implements permission inheritance from parent folders to child dashboards and subfolders. This function queries the folder service to get ancestors and builds a chain of inherited permission scopes.\\n\\n`pkg/services/searchV2/auth.go` uses inherited scopes for search result filtering, checking permissions across the folder hierarchy.\\n\\n`pkg/api/annotations.go` applies inherited scopes when resolving permissions for annotations linked to dashboards.\\n\\n## Folder Hierarchy Support\\n`pkg/services/folder/service.go` and `pkg/services/folder/model.go` provide folder hierarchy operations. The folder service's `GetParents()` method is used by `GetInheritedScopes()` to walk up the folder tree and collect inherited permission scopes.\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to:\\n1. Define granular permission actions mapped to three role tiers\\n2. Enforce permissions via middleware on all endpoints\\n3. Allow per-resource permission overrides for users, teams, and basic roles\\n4. Inherit permissions from parent folders to contained resources\\n5. Validate and update permissions through a centralized permissions service\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
